I want a new summary outlining these mission essential functions for a different department::

MEFs encompass those critical areas of business that must continue even during a disruption event. These essential business functions must be performed to achieve Bus Operations’ mission. Each essential function, in turn, is supported by critical processes or services that are provided to the public or other departments within Metro. Essential functions are those that enable the department to provide vital services, maintain Metro’s good name, generate revenue, minimize legal exposure, protect life and property, or ensure the well-being of ridership and citizens.
A recovery time objective (RTO) is the amount of time in which systems, processes, services, or functions must be restored to acceptable levels to ensure the continuation of MEFs.
The following are MEFs for Bus Operations:
•	Facilities Maintenance & Bus Operations
o	Maintain bus communications.
o	Maintain non-revenue fleet.
o	Maintain revenue fleet.
o	Maintain HVAC system.
o	Maintain bus stops.
o	Fuel buses, non-revenue vehicles, and heavy-duty trucks.
•	Transportation
o	Operate Buses
2025-02-27 20:15:48 | 2024 Rail Operations COOP Summary
Purpose and Scope
The Los Angeles County Metropolitan Transportation Authority (Metro) developed this Continuity of Operations Plan (COOP) to ensure the continued execution of Mission Essential Functions (MEFs) during and after disruptive events. The plan aligns with federal and state guidelines, including NIMS, SEMS, and the California Government Code.
COOP Activation (Triggers)
The Continuity of Operations Plan (COOP) is activated when incidents disrupt Metro and Rail operations by impairing infrastructure, staffing, or technology for a significant period. Activation depends on whether the incident occurs with or without prior notice.
•	Incidents with Notice (e.g., severe weather, pandemics, planned events, labor strikes) allow for preparation and coordination among leadership, ensuring continuity measures are in place before disruptions occur.
•	Incidents without Notice (e.g., earthquakes, fires, power outages, terrorist events) require immediate response, often delaying activation due to assessment needs. Situational awareness from security, safety, and IT teams is critical in guiding response efforts.
The COOP Manager, in coordination with department leadership and Rail Operations Senior Leadership, oversees activation, communication, and operational continuity to minimize service disruptions.
Key Objectives
•	Ensure the continuity of essential rail services during emergencies.
•	Protect Metro’s facilities, assets, personnel, and infrastructure.
•	Minimize operational disruptions and financial losses.
•	Establish clear communication and coordination among Metro teams.
•	Support timely recovery and reconstitution of operations.
Mission Essential Functions (MEFs)
The following core functions must be maintained:
Rail Facilities Maintenance
•	Inspect and maintain stations, structures, and shop equipment
Rail Fleet Services
•	Inspect and maintain rail cars
•	Maintain Railcars for Revenue Service
•	Ensure Division and Shop Equipment Readiness
•	M3 Maintenance of records at all Divisions.

Continued on next page

Rail Transportation
•	Command and control of train movement
•	Move people via rail
Wayside Systems (Signals, Tracks, Power, Communications, SCADA, Wayside Systems)
•	Maintain tracks
•	Maintain Grade Crossings and Train Control system (Interlockings, Switches, Signals, Track Circuits, Cab Speed Network, Communication Network to SCADA
•	Maintain radio communication between trains and control center
•	Inspect and maintain third rail system, overhead catenary lines, substation, and all power in rail stations
•	Maintain SCADA system communications between Wayside Systems and Control Center
Phases of COOP Implementation
1.	Readiness & Preparedness: Identifying critical personnel, conducting training, and preparing facilities.
2.	Activation & Relocation: Mobilizing emergency response teams, assessing damage, and activating backup sites.
3.	Continuity Operations: Executing MEFs using alternate facilities or remote operations.
4.	Reconstitution & Recovery: Returning to normal operations, assessing response effectiveness, and implementing improvements.
Emergency Response
•	The COOP Manager oversees activation and coordination with Metro’s Emergency Management Department (EMD).
•	Incidents may require telework, facility relocation, devolution of authority, or temporary service suspension.
•	The Continuity Management Group (CMG) manages personnel assignments and recovery strategies.
Key Contacts During Emergencies:
•	Metro Employee Emergency Hotline: (877) 955-5234
•	Emergency Operations Center (EOC): (213) 922-8899
•	COOP Manager (Conan Cheung): (213) 418-3034

Authorized Activation Personnel 
Position/Title 	Name	Office Phone:	Email:
Chief Operations Officer (COO)*	Conan Cheung	2134183034	CheungC@metro.net
Deputy COO	Edna Stanley	2139224084	StanleyE@metro.net
Deputy COO	Matthew Dake	2139224061	DakeM@metro.net
Deputy COO	Errol Taylor	2139223227	TayloeE@metro.net
*During incident response, the COO assumes the role of COOP Manager but may delegate this role to a Deputy COO if necessary.

One of the main processes of the site is saving 'bubbles' to an azure database. I can load them alright but sometimes the saving doesn't work. Here's the function that loads the bubbles that seems to work well::

app.get('/loadBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      const userId = decoded.id; // Assuming userId is included in your token
      const pool = await getConnection();
      const bubblesResult = await pool.request()
        .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
        .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

      await pool.close(); // Close the connection
      res.json({
        success: true,
        bubbles: bubblesResult.recordset // Send the users bubbles
      });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Internal server error' });
    }
  } else {
    res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
});

Here's the saving function that doesn't work everytime (sometimes it does tho so idk)

app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.session.userId; // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session
  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles; // Expecting bubbles to be an array of objects

  if (!userId || !Array.isArray(bubbles)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });
  }

  try {
    const pool = await getConnection();
    // Clear existing bubbles for this user if needed (optional)
    await pool.request()
      .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
      .query('DELETE FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

    // Insert each bubble into the database
    for (const bubble of bubbles) {
      const { group, text } = bubble;
      await pool.request()
        .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
        .input('text', sql.NVarChar, text)
        .input('group', sql.NVarChar, group)
        .query('INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, [group]) VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)');
    }

    await pool.close(); // Close the connection
    res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });
  }
});

2025-02-20 21:25:27 | Criteria for COOP Activation and Relocation Decisions
The COOP Manager or designated Rail personnel will activate the COOP in response to any of the incidents or situations based on the following criteria:

1.	The incident or situation will disrupt Metro operations and/or Rail operations by impairing infrastructure, staffing, or technology.
2.	The impairment will last for a considerable length of time.

The activation procedure depends on the amount of notification given, which greatly changes the ability to prepare, plan, and activate the COOP. The activation will be executed in one of two primary ways:
•	Incidents with notice
•	Incidents without notice
 


Incidents with notice include large-scale weather events, pandemics or biohazards, forewarned terrorist attacks, large-scale planned events such as conventions, sporting and cultural events, and labor strikes. Metro’s Emergency Management and other department executive leadership monitor these incidents with notice.

The COOP Manager communicates with department leadership about agency preparations and determines continuity actions in coordination with the Board, CEO, and designated Rail Personnel, and others as deemed necessary.

Leading up to such an event, all teams shall communicate actions, activities, conditions, and concerns to the COOP Manager, who will then funnel appropriate information to the Senior Leadership team (SLT) or Executive Staff.

The Rail Operations SLT is responsible for anticipating impacts and making decisions to manage and continue operations. The team leaders are fully responsible and accountable for managing operations throughout the Incident.

Incidents without notice are unplanned and generally unrelated to weather, such as major earthquakes, building fires, utility outages, disruptions, and breakdowns. Law enforcement and terrorist events often occur without notice. Incidents without notice do not allow time to consider possible impacts or activate planning and response procedures in advance. Many incidents without notice require immediate action by departments to reduce impacts to staff, facilities, and processes.

During the early stages of an incident without notice, accurate and timely situational awareness is vitally important. Situational awareness will usually be provided by various staff with expertise or proximity to the subject causing the impact. This may include security, building management, real estate, safety management, and information technology.

Initial response to an incident without notice may be delayed by the preliminary site assessment/investigation. Such an investigation can require time to determine the nature of the situation and the appropriate actions. Each incident is unique.

2025-02-19 18:53:25 | import os
import docx

def extract_sections_from_docx(docx_path):
    doc = docx.Document(docx_path)
    sections = []
    current_section = None
    current_content = []
    current_table_data = []
    
    # Process paragraphs and headings
    for para in doc.paragraphs:
        # Check for headings (we assume all headings are section titles)
        if para.style.name.startswith("Heading"):  
            # If there's an existing section, add it to sections
            if current_section:
                sections.append((current_section, current_content, current_table_data))
            current_section = para.text.strip()  # Set new section title
            current_content = []  # Reset content for the new section
            current_table_data = []  # Reset table data for the new section
        else:  # Regular content under the section
            current_content.append(para.text.strip())
        
    # Now process tables and add them to their respective section
    for table in doc.tables:
        table_row_data = []
        for row in table.rows:
            row_data = [cell.text.strip() for cell in row.cells]
            table_row_data.append(" | ".join(row_data))  # Convert to Markdown table row
        
        if table_row_data:
            current_table_data.append(table_row_data)  # Store table data for current section
    
    # Add the last section if exists
    if current_section:
        sections.append((current_section, current_content, current_table_data))

    return sections

def sanitize_filename(name):
    return name.replace(":", "_").replace("/", "_").replace("\\", "_")

def save_sections_to_md(output_folder, sections):
    if not os.path.exists(output_folder):
        os.makedirs(output_folder)

    for section, content, table_data in sections:
        section_folder = os.path.join(output_folder, sanitize_filename(section))
        os.makedirs(section_folder, exist_ok=True)

        # Save the main section content in a .md file
        section_filename = sanitize_filename(section) + ".md"
        section_file_path = os.path.join(section_folder, section_filename)
        with open(section_file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            f.write("# " + section + "\n\n")
            f.write("\n".join(content))

        # Save each table in a separate .md file inside the section's folder
        for idx, table in enumerate(table_data):
            table_filename = f"table_{idx+1}.md"
            table_file_path = os.path.join(section_folder, table_filename)
            with open(table_file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write("**Table Data:**\n")
                f.write("\n".join(table))  # Each table row is joined by newline

def process_docx(docx_path, output_folder):
    sections = extract_sections_from_docx(docx_path)
    save_sections_to_md(output_folder, sections)
    print(f"Processed and saved to {output_folder}")

# Example usage:
docx_file = r"L:\IV. Emergency Operations Plans (EOP)\Continuity Of Operations Plans (COOP)\2023-2024\BUS\2022 Bus Ops  COOP_DRAFT.docx"
output_dir = r"C:\Bus_Coop_Sectioned"
process_docx(docx_file, output_dir)

2025-02-19 00:01:21 | import os
import docx
import re

def extract_sections_from_docx(docx_path):
    doc = docx.Document(docx_path)
    sections = {}
    current_section = None
    current_subsections = []
    current_content = []

    for para in doc.paragraphs:
        if para.style.name.startswith("Heading 1"):  # Main Section
            if current_section:
                sections[current_section] = current_subsections
            current_section = para.text.strip()
            current_subsections = []
        elif para.style.name.startswith("Heading 2"):  # Subsection
            if current_content:
                current_subsections.append((current_subsection, current_content))
            current_subsection = para.text.strip()
            current_content = []
        else:  # Regular content
            current_content.append(para.text.strip())

    # Capture last section
    if current_section:
        sections[current_section] = current_subsections

    # Extract tables
    for table in doc.tables:
        table_data = []
        for row in table.rows:
            row_data = [cell.text.strip() for cell in row.cells]
            table_data.append(" | ".join(row_data))  # Convert to Markdown table row

        if table_data:
            table_text = "\n".join(table_data)
            if current_content:
                current_content.append("\n**Table Data:**\n" + table_text)
            else:
                current_content = ["\n**Table Data:**\n" + table_text]

    return sections

def sanitize_filename(name):
    return name.replace(":", "_").replace("/", "_").replace("\\", "_")

def save_sections_to_md(output_folder, sections):
    if not os.path.exists(output_folder):
        os.makedirs(output_folder)

    for section, subsections in sections.items():
        section_folder = os.path.join(output_folder, sanitize_filename(section))
        os.makedirs(section_folder, exist_ok=True)
        
        for subsection, content in subsections:
            file_path = os.path.join(section_folder, sanitize_filename(subsection) + ".md")
            with open(file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write("# " + subsection + "\n\n" + "\n".join(content))

def process_docx(docx_path, output_folder):
    sections = extract_sections_from_docx(docx_path)
    save_sections_to_md(output_folder, sections)
    print(f"Processed and saved to {output_folder}")

# Example usage:
docx_file = r"L:\IV. Emergency Operations Plans (EOP)\Continuity Of Operations Plans (COOP)\2023-2024\BUS\2022 Bus Ops  COOP_DRAFT.docx" 
output_dir = r"C:\Bus_Coop_Sectioned"
process_docx(docx_file, output_dir)

def sanitize_filename(name):
    return name.replace(":", "_").replace("/", "_").replace("\\", "_")

def save_sections_to_md(output_folder, sections):
    if not os.path.exists(output_folder):
        os.makedirs(output_folder)

    for section, subsections in sections.items():
        section_folder = os.path.join(output_folder, sanitize_filename(section))
        os.makedirs(section_folder, exist_ok=True)
        
        for subsection, content in subsections:
            file_path = os.path.join(section_folder, sanitize_filename(subsection) + ".md")
            with open(file_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
                f.write("# " + subsection + "\n\n" + "\n".join(content))

def process_docx(docx_path, output_folder):
    sections = extract_sections_from_docx(docx_path)
    save_sections_to_md(output_folder, sections)
    print(f"Processed and saved to {output_folder}")

# Example usage:
docx_file = r"L:\IV. Emergency Operations Plans (EOP)\Continuity Of Operations Plans (COOP)\2023-2024\BUS\2022 Bus Ops  COOP_DRAFT.docx" 
output_dir = r"C:\Bus_Coop_Sectioned"
process_docx(docx_file, output_dir)

2025-02-13 23:01:22 | import os

def replicate_folder_structure(source_dir, destination_dir):
    """
    Recursively replicates the folder structure from source_dir to destination_dir.
    """
    # Loop through the directory structure of the source folder
    
    if os.name == "nt":  # Windows only
        source_dir = f"\\\\?\\{source_dir}"
        destination_dir = f"\\\\?\\{destination_dir}"
    
    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(source_dir):
        # Calculate the relative path of the current folder
        relative_path = os.path.relpath(root, source_dir)
        
        # Create the corresponding destination folder
        destination_folder = os.path.join(destination_dir, relative_path)
        if not os.path.exists(destination_folder):
            os.makedirs(destination_folder)
            print(f"Created folder: {destination_folder}")
        
        # If you want to see the files, but we're not doing anything with them yet:
        for file in files:
            # You could optionally handle files here, but this script is only concerned with folders
            pass

# Example usage:
source_path = r"L:"  # Replace with the actual path to your drive

    os.makedirs(destination_path)

2025-02-14 00:28:47 | import os
import shutil
import pypandoc  # Install with: pip install pypandoc

def convert_to_md(source_file, destination_file):
    """Converts a file to Markdown format using Pandoc, if supported."""
    try:
        output = pypandoc.convert_file(source_file, 'markdown')
        with open(destination_file, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            f.write(output)
        print(f"Converted: {source_file} -> {destination_file}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Skipping {source_file} (Error: {e})")

def copy_and_convert_files(source_dir, destination_dir):
    """
    Copies all supported files from source_dir to destination_dir, converting them to .md.
    """
    source_dir = os.path.abspath(source_dir)
    destination_dir = os.path.abspath(destination_dir)

    # Apply \\?\ for long paths if on Windows
    if os.name == "nt":
        if not source_dir.startswith("\\\\?\\"):
            source_dir = f"\\\\?\\{source_dir}"
        if not destination_dir.startswith("\\\\?\\"):
            destination_dir = f"\\\\?\\{destination_dir}"

    for root, _, files in os.walk(source_dir):
        # Get the relative path
        relative_path = os.path.relpath(root, source_dir)
        destination_folder = os.path.join(destination_dir, relative_path)

        # Ensure the destination folder exists
        os.makedirs(destination_folder, exist_ok=True)

        for file in files:
            source_file = os.path.join(root, file)

            # Determine destination file name with .md extension
            base_name, ext = os.path.splitext(file)
            destination_file = os.path.join(destination_folder, base_name + ".md")

            if ext.lower() in [".txt", ".pdf", ".docx", ".html"]:  # Supported formats
                convert_to_md(source_file, destination_file)
            else:
                print(f"Skipping unsupported file: {source_file}")

# Example usage
source_path = r"C:\test1"  # Make sure it's correct
destination_path = r"C:\Users\WeisburgC\OneDrive - Los Angeles County Metropolitan Transportation Authority\Documents\coding messarounds\L_Copy"

copy_and_convert_files(source_path, destination_path)

2025-02-13 17:07:59 | def pdf_to_csv(pdf_path, csv_path):
    """Extract text from the first page of a PDF and save it as a CSV file."""
    try:
        # Open the PDF file
        doc = fitz.open(pdf_path)
        
        # Extract text from the first page
        if len(doc) > 0:
            text = doc[0].get_text("text")
        else:
            print("PDF is empty.")
            return
        
        # Split text into lines
        lines = text.split('\n')
        
        # Write to CSV file
        with open(csv_path, mode='w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as file:
            writer = csv.writer(file)
            for line in lines:
                writer.writerow([line])  # Each line as a single column entry
        
        print(f"CSV file saved at {csv_path}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error: {e}")

# Example usage

2025-02-13 17:54:32 | import fitz  # PyMuPDF
import csv

def pdf_to_csv(pdf_path, csv_path):
    """Extract text from the first page of a PDF and save it as a CSV file."""
    try:
        # Open the PDF file
        doc = fitz.open(pdf_path)
        
        # Extract text from the first page
        if len(doc) > 0:
            text = doc[0].get_text("text")
        else:
            print("PDF is empty.")
            return
        
        # Split text into lines
        lines = text.split('\n')
        
        # Write to CSV file
        with open(csv_path, mode='w', newline='', encoding='utf-8') as file:
            writer = csv.writer(file)
            for line in lines:
                writer.writerow([line])  # Each line as a single column entry
        
        print(f"CSV file saved at {csv_path}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error: {e}")

# Example usage
pdf_to_csv("input.pdf", "output.csv")

function LogoWithLink({ link, icon }: { link: string; icon: ReactElement }) {
  return (
    <div className="">
      <a

        href={link}
        target="_blank"

      >
        {icon}

    </div>
  );
}

}) {

        <div className="p-3 pt-8">

  );

      </div>
    </div>
  );

2024-12-19 02:38:27 | import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const MyComponent = () => {
  // State to store screen width and height
  const [screenSize, setScreenSize] = useState({
    width: window.innerWidth,
    height: window.innerHeight
  });

  // Update screenSize on window resize
  useEffect(() => {
    const handleResize = () => {
      setScreenSize({
        width: window.innerWidth,
        height: window.innerHeight
      });
    };

    // Event listener for window resize
    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);

    // Clean up event listener on unmount
    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
  }, []);

  // Use screen width and height to conditionally render
  const isDesktop = screenSize.width >= 1024; // Adjust based on your desktop breakpoint
  const isMobile = screenSize.width < 1024;  // Adjust based on your mobile breakpoint

  return (
    <main className="flex flex-row items-center justify-center w-full min-h-screen flex-1 px-8 gap-6 text-start">
      {/* Conditional rendering based on screen size */}
      {isDesktop && (
        <div className="z-10 bg-opacity-0 relative flex flex-col min-h-screen h-full justify-center items-start">
          {/* Desktop-specific content */}
        </div>
      )}

      {isMobile && (
        <div className="absolute top-0 left-0 w-full px-4 py-10 z-10 bg-transparent flex justify-center items-center">
          {/* Mobile-specific content */}
        </div>
      )}
    </main>
  );
};

export default MyComponent;

I am an analytical explorer. I am naturally curious about the patterns in the world around me, especially when it comes to numbers and data and how those can be used to strategize and make informed decisions. Early in life, I was drawn to the beauty of activities like chess and music that required deep pattern recognition within a playful and low-stakes environment. 2024-12-14 15:12:24 | Before I became a career coach I was, at times, a job seeker. I was always a bit puzzled by the idea that I should “ask for the job” at the end of an interview.
How would that sound? “Will you give me this job, please?” Laughable. Depending on the tone of voice, this could sound either like begging or an impatient whine! Then I imagined just bluntly saying, “I want this job.” Better, but abrupt.
And what were they supposed to answer? “Oh, well, now that you ask, sure!” Yeah, right!
A Pet Peeve of Interviewers: “I can’t tell whether he’s interested!”
What it’s really about is this: at the end of any interview, the interviewer needs to know you’re seriously interested in moving forward in the process. If you’re not, they don’t want to waste time on further discussions.
They can’t assume you’re interested just because you showed up for the interview. People often interview for jobs they’re not very interested in, either because the role might turn out to be better than it sounded in the posting, or even just for practice.
If this is the final interview before consideration of an offer, they need to know you want the job. Even if you’re still not sure the salary or specifics are going meet your requirements, if the job itself is something you’d like to do, say so. The rest can often be negotiated.
How to Ask for the Job: Examples
This is how asking for the job might sound.
	•	“Based on everything I’ve heard and seen, it’s pretty clear to me that I want this job. With my strategic planning and team building skills, I can really see myself helping this program grow to its potential.”
	•	“I know you have a process so I won’t expect an answer right now, but I’d really like to join your team. Please let me know if you need anything else from me.”
	•	“I want you to know that I’m very interested in taking on this role, and I hope you’ll be making me an offer. Thanks again for meeting with me.”
You may have heard of bolder ways of asking, like “So, have I got the job?” In sales an approach like this may be called for in order to demonstrate your aggressive sales closing technique, but for most roles a gentler statement like those above is best, in order to avoid putting the interviewer on the spot.
A Solvable Problem: Fearing What You’ll Hear
Job seekers are quite understandably anxious about sticking their necks out by asking for the job. If you ask yourself why, you may notice that you’re worried about what you’ll hear in response. So let’s get you prepared for the possibilities.
First, it’s highly unlikely that they’re going to say no right on the spot. If this did happen you could say calmly, “Well, that’s a bit of a surprise.” (Smile.) “I’m interested in knowing your reasons for that decision.”
The much more likely response is: “That’s good to know, because we’re very interested in you as well, and we’ll get back to you within the next (few days, couple of weeks, etc.).” You then say something like “Great!” Pretty do-able, really.
Now remember, you’re not a mind reader. Decide right now that whatever they say, you’ll accept it with an open mind and a confident smile. Practice that in your mind, or even in a mirror. After you’ve done that you may find that you’re feeling less shy about saying you want the job.
I hope the above gives you a more workable view of how to ask for the job at the end of your job interviews. For more tips, read my post on what to say at the end of the interview.

2024-11-04 07:42:54 | Prompt::: All too often, companies hire outside consultants to suggest ways for the company to operate more efficiently. If companies were to spend more time listening to their own employees, such consultants would be unnecessary.
Write a response in which you discuss the extent to which you agree or disagree with these statements and explain your reasoning for the position you take. In developing and supporting your position, you should consider ways in which the statements might or might not hold true and explain how these considerations shape your position.


Response::: When a business hires an outside consultant for advice regarding operations, employees may feel disgruntled because they believe they know the business and possible inefficiencies better than any outside source. However, independent help offers a unique perspective and role that does provide an important and valuable service to businesses because they may have wider experience within an industry, they have the right incentive structure, and they have a wider knowledge for tools that a business could use to become more efficient.
Consultants have worked with many business, often within the same industry, and they can provide insight to how other businesses are working well. When a consultant is moving quickly between businesses, they get this unique perspective of what is happening on a larger scale and know what sort of trends and improvements are being made on the wider scale. Employees may know the individual business better, but an outside consultant knows the industry better. Consider a young entrepreneur that is forming a business within the landscaping industry. The advivce that he needs to grow the business will not lie within his employees who are cutting grass and planting bushes all day. He needs help from someone older and more experienced within the industry- someone who understands the sales process better or may have tips on where to find cheaper supplies. Some of that knowledge may lie within the employees too, but it is far likelier to be within someone that has tested the advice and struggled through the same things. 
Consultants are also important because their incentives are aligned in the right way. Someone within the company is paid to do a certain role, perhaps to fix irragation systems. That person may notice ways that the business might function better, but often there is no incentive for that person to actually fix the problem. They are paid the same whether they fix the problem or not. However, a consultant is paid to find and solve those problems. The consultant has the right incentive to address problems within a company. 
Finally, consultants have access to a wider knowledge of tools available to businesses. If there is an issue with the scheduling system for a service company, employees may not know of any other options, but a consultant might. 
Consultants are very useful to businesses.

2024-10-02 02:32:07 | const express = require('express');
const session = require('express-session');
const sql = require('mssql');
const path = require('path');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const cookieParser = require('cookie-parser');

const app = express();

// Middleware for handling POST data
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
app.use(express.json());
app.use(cookieParser()); // Middleware to parse cookies

// Serve static files from bubbleSiteFiles directory
app.use('/bubbles', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles')));

require('dotenv').config();

// SQL Server configuration
const poolConfig = {
  user: process.env.DB_USER,              // Use environment variable
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,      // Use environment variable
  server: process.env.DB_SERVER,          // Use environment variable
  database: process.env.DB_DATABASE,      // Use environment variable
  options: {
    encrypt: true, // Set to true if using Azure
    trustServerCertificate: false, // Set to true for local testing, if necessary
    enableArithAbort: true, // Required for Azure SQL
  },
};

// JWT secret key
const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET; // Use environment variable

// Create a connection pool
const poolPromise = new sql.ConnectionPool(poolConfig)
  .connect()
  .then(pool => {
    console.log('Connected to MSSQL');
    return pool;
  })
  .catch(err => {
    console.error('Database connection failed: ', err);
  });
poolPromise.catch(err => {
  console.error('Production pool error: ', err.message);
});

// Session middleware setup
app.use(session({
  secret: JWT_SECRET, // Replace with your secret key
  resave: false,
  saveUninitialized: true,
  cookie: { secure: false } // Set to true if using HTTPS
}));

app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.redirect('/login'); // Redirects root URL to the login page
});

// User registration route
app.post('/register', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    await pool.request()
      .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)
      .input('hashedPassword', sql.NVarChar, hashedPassword)
      .query('INSERT INTO Users (username, password) VALUES (@username, @hashedPassword)');
    res.redirect('/login');
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    res.status(500).send('Registration failed.');
  }
});

// User login route
app.post('/login', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request()
      .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)
      .query('SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = @username');
    if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
      const user = result.recordset[0];
      const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);
      if (passwordMatch) {
        const token = jwt.sign({ username: user.username, id: user.id }, JWT_SECRET);
        req.session.userId = user.id; // Store user ID in session
        res.cookie('authToken', token);
        res.redirect('/bubbles');
      } else {
        res.status(400).send('Invalid password.');
      }
    } else {

2024-10-02 22:42:15 | const express = require('express');
const session = require('express-session');
const sql = require('mssql');
const path = require('path');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const cookieParser = require('cookie-parser');

const app = express(); 

// Middleware for handling POST data
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
app.use(express.json());
app.use(cookieParser()); // Middleware to parse cookies

// Serve static files from bubbleSiteFiles directory
app.use('/bubbles', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles')));

require('dotenv').config();
console.log('DB Config:', {
  user: process.env.DB_USER,
  server: process.env.DB_SERVER,
  database: process.env.DB_DATABASE,
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD
});
// SQL Server configuration
const poolConfig = {
  user: process.env.DB_USER,              // Use environment variable
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,      // Use environment variable
  server: process.env.DB_SERVER,          // Use environment variable
  database: process.env.DB_DATABASE,      // Use environment variable
  options: {
    encrypt: true, // Set to true if using Azure
    trustServerCertificate: false, // Set to true for local testing, if necessary
    enableArithAbort: true, // Required for Azure SQL
  },
  connectionTimeout: 30000, // Set timeout to 30 seconds
  requestTimeout: 30000     // Optional: Increase request timeout as well
};

// JWT secret key
const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET; // Use environment variable

// Create a connection pool
const poolPromise = new sql.ConnectionPool(poolConfig)
  .connect()
  .then(pool => {
    console.log('Connected to MSSQL');
    return pool;
  })
  .catch(err => {
    console.error('Database connection failed: ', err);
  });
poolPromise.catch(err => {
  console.error('Production pool error: ', err.message);
});

// Session middleware setup
app.use(session({
  secret: JWT_SECRET, // Replace with your secret key
  resave: false,
  saveUninitialized: true,
  cookie: { secure: false } // Set to true if using HTTPS
}));

app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.redirect('/login'); // Redirects root URL to the login page
});

// User registration route
app.post('/register', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    await pool.request()
      .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)
      .input('hashedPassword', sql.NVarChar, hashedPassword)
      .query('INSERT INTO Users (username, password) VALUES (@username, @hashedPassword)');
    res.redirect('/login');
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    res.status(500).send('Registration failed.');
  }
});
app.get('/clear-sessions', (req, res) => {
  req.sessionStore.all((err, sessions) => {
    if (err) {
      return res.status(500).send('Error clearing sessions.');
    }
    
    // Iterate through all sessions and destroy them
    for (let sessionId in sessions) {
      req.sessionStore.destroy(sessionId, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error(`Failed to destroy session ${sessionId}:`, err);
        }
      });
    }
    
    res.send('All sessions cleared.');
  });
});
// User login route
app.post('/login', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request()
      .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)
      .query('SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = @username');
    if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
      const user = result.recordset[0];
      const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);
      if (passwordMatch) {
        const token = jwt.sign({ username: user.username, id: user.id }, JWT_SECRET);
        req.session.userId = user.id; // Store user ID in session
        res.cookie('authToken', token);
        res.redirect('/bubbles');
      } else {
        res.status(400).send('Invalid password.');
      }
    } else {
      res.status(400).send('User not found.');
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    res.status(500).send('Login failed.');
  }
});

// Route to serve the bubble site after login
app.get('/bubbles', (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles', 'index.html'));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.redirect('/login');
    }
  } else {
    res.redirect('/login');
  }
});

// Route to save bubble DOM structure to SQL database
app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.session.userId; // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session
  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles; // Expecting bubbles to be an array of objects
  console.log(userId, bubbles);

  if (!userId || !Array.isArray(bubbles)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });
  }

  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    // Clear existing bubbles for this user if needed (optional)
    await pool.request()
      .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
      .query('DELETE FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

    // Insert each bubble into the database
    for (const bubble of bubbles) {
      const { group, text } = bubble;
      await pool.request()
        .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
        .input('text', sql.NVarChar, text)
        .input('group', sql.NVarChar, group)
        .query('INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, [group]) VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)');
    }

    res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });
  }
});

// Endpoint to load user's bubbles
app.get('/loadBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      const userId = decoded.id; // Assuming userId is included in your token
      const pool = await poolPromise;
      const bubblesResult = await pool.request()
        .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
        .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

      res.json({
        success: true,
        bubbles: bubblesResult.recordset // Send the user's bubbles
      });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Internal server error' });
    }
  } else {
    res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
});

// Serve the login page
app.get('/login', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));
});

// Route to retrieve and print Users table
app.get('/users', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request().query('SELECT * FROM Users');
    console.log(result.recordset);
    res.json(result.recordset);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving users.' });
  }
});

// Route to retrieve all bubbles associated with user with id=3
app.get('/userbubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = 3; // You can replace this with a dynamic value if needed

  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request()
      .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
      .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

    if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
      res.json(result.recordset);
    } else {
      res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'No bubbles found for this user.' });
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving bubbles.' });
  }
});

// const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// app.listen(PORT, () => {
//     console.log(`Server is running on http://localhost:${PORT}`);
// });
module.exports= app;

const session = require('express-session');
const sql = require('mssql');

const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');

app.use(express.json());
app.use(cookieParser()); // Middleware to parse cookies

  user: process.env.DB_USER,              // Use environment variable
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,      // Use environment variable
  server: process.env.DB_SERVER,          // Use environment variable
  database: process.env.DB_DATABASE,      // Use environment variable
  options: {
    encrypt: true, // Set to true if using Azure
    trustServerCertificate: false, // Set to true for local testing, if necessary
    enableArithAbort: true, // Required for Azure SQL
  },
  connectionTimeout: 30000, // Set timeout to 30 seconds
  requestTimeout: 30000     // Optional: Increase request timeout as well
};

// JWT secret key
const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET; // Use environment variable

// Create a connection pool
const poolPromise = new sql.ConnectionPool(poolConfig)
  .connect()
  .then(pool => {
    console.log('Connected to MSSQL');
    return pool;
  })
  .catch(err => {
    console.error('Database connection failed: ', err);
  });
poolPromise.catch(err => {
  console.error('Production pool error: ', err.message);
});

// Session middleware setup
app.use(session({
  secret: JWT_SECRET, // Replace with your secret key
  resave: false,
  saveUninitialized: true,
  cookie: { secure: false } // Set to true if using HTTPS
}));

app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.redirect('/login'); // Redirects root URL to the login page
});

// User registration route
app.post('/register', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    await pool.request()
      .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)
      .input('hashedPassword', sql.NVarChar, hashedPassword)
      .query('INSERT INTO Users (username, password) VALUES (@username, @hashedPassword)');
    res.redirect('/login');
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    res.status(500).send('Registration failed.');
  }
});
app.get('/clear-sessions', (req, res) => {
  req.sessionStore.all((err, sessions) => {
    if (err) {
      return res.status(500).send('Error clearing sessions.');
    }
    
    // Iterate through all sessions and destroy them
    for (let sessionId in sessions) {
      req.sessionStore.destroy(sessionId, (err) => {
        if (err) {
          console.error(`Failed to destroy session ${sessionId}:`, err);
        }
      });
    }
    
    res.send('All sessions cleared.');
  });
});
app.get('/test-connection', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    res.json({ success: true, message: 'Connection successful' });
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('Connection error:', err);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, error: err.message });

});

// User login route
app.post('/login', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request()
      .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)
      .query('SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = @username');
    if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
      const user = result.recordset[0];
      const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);
      if (passwordMatch) {
        const token = jwt.sign({ username: user.username, id: user.id }, JWT_SECRET);
        req.session.userId = user.id; // Store user ID in session
        res.cookie('authToken', token);
        res.redirect('/bubbles');
      } else {
        res.status(400).send('Invalid password.');
      }
    } else {
      res.status(400).send('User not found.');
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    res.status(500).send('Login failed.');
  }
});

// Route to serve the bubble site after login
app.get('/bubbles', (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles', 'index.html'));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.redirect('/login');
    }
  } else {
    res.redirect('/login');
  }
});

// Route to save bubble DOM structure to SQL database
app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.session.userId; // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session
  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles; // Expecting bubbles to be an array of objects
  console.log(userId, bubbles);

  if (!userId || !Array.isArray(bubbles)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });
  }

  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    // Clear existing bubbles for this user if needed (optional)
    await pool.request()
      .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
      .query('DELETE FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

    // Insert each bubble into the database
    for (const bubble of bubbles) {
      const { group, text } = bubble;
      await pool.request()
        .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
        .input('text', sql.NVarChar, text)
        .input('group', sql.NVarChar, group)
        .query('INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, [group]) VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)');
    }

    res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });
  }
});

// Endpoint to load user's bubbles
app.get('/loadBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      const userId = decoded.id; // Assuming userId is included in your token
      const pool = await poolPromise;
      const bubblesResult = await pool.request()
        .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
        .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

      res.json({
        success: true,
        bubbles: bubblesResult.recordset // Send the user's bubbles
      });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Internal server error' });
    }
  } else {
    res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
});

// Serve the login page
app.get('/login', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));
});

  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request().query('SELECT * FROM Users');
    console.log(result.recordset);
    res.json(result.recordset);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving users.' });
  }
});

// Route to retrieve all bubbles associated with user with id=3
app.get('/userbubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = 3; // You can replace this with a dynamic value if needed

  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request()
      .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
      .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

    if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
      res.json(result.recordset);
    } else {
      res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'No bubbles found for this user.' });
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving bubbles.' });
  }
});

2024-09-21 23:41:28 |  function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {
    textSpan.addEventListener('click', function () {
        const inputField = document.createElement('input');
        inputField.type = 'text';
        inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  // Set the input's value to current text
        textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  // Replace text with input field
        inputField.focus();  // Automatically focus on the input

        inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {
            updateText();
        });

        // Listen for the Enter key
        inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                updateText();
            }
        });

        function updateText() {
            textSpan.innerText = inputField.value || "Click to Edit";  // Update textSpan with new input value
            inputField.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Replace input with updated text
        }
    });
}

2024-09-22 03:14:34 | function createBubble() {
    const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!groupName) return;

    let group = groups[groupName];

    if (!group) {
        const color = getRandomColor(); // Generate a new color for the group
        group = createGroup(groupName, color);
        groups[groupName] = group; // Store the group in the groups object
        document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group); // Add the group to the container
    }

    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');
    newBubble.classList.add('bubble');
    newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.style.borderColor; // Set the bubble color
    newBubble.style.width = '50px';
    newBubble.style.height = '50px';
    newBubble.style.borderRadius = '10px'; // Rounded corners
    newBubble.style.margin = '5px'; // Spacing between bubbles
    newBubble.style.position = 'absolute'; // Ensure bubbles can be positioned
    newBubble.style.cursor = 'move'; // Change cursor to indicate draggable
    
    // Create a span for editable text
    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
    textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit"; // Default text
    textSpan.style.display = 'block'; // Display block for line breaks
    textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center'; // Center text

    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan); // Add the text span to the bubble
    group.appendChild(newBubble); // Add the new bubble to the group

    // Make the bubble editable
    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);

    // Call functions for dragging (if applicable)
    makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);
}

function createGroup(name, color) {
    const groupDiv = document.createElement('div');
    groupDiv.classList.add('group');
    groupDiv.style.border = `2px solid ${color}`; // Set border color

    groupDiv.style.margin = '10px'; // Add some margin for spacing

    const groupTitle = document.createElement('h3');
    groupTitle.innerText = name;

}

2024-09-22 21:13:04 | Alright lets get back to it. So something is not working with the bubbles. They won't drag now. Lets go back to the initiation of the groups. When using the flex function, are the positions of these grids saved?

2024-09-22 21:16:33 | function makeBubbleDraggable(bubble) {
    bubble.addEventListener('mousedown', function (event) {
        offsetX = event.clientX - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().left; // Calculate horizontal offset
        offsetY = event.clientY - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().top; // Calculate vertical offset

        function mouseMoveHandler(e) {
            bubble.style.position = 'absolute'; // Set position to absolute
            bubble.style.left = `${e.clientX - offsetX}px`; // Use the offset
            bubble.style.top = `${e.clientY - offsetY}px`; // Use the offset
        }

        function mouseUpHandler() {
            document.removeEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);
            document.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);
        }

        document.addEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);
        document.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);
    });
}
2024-09-22 21:18:49 | yeah they wont drag

2024-09-22 21:19:03 | yeah they wont drag

2024-09-22 21:20:37 | const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');
const createBubbleBtn = document.getElementById('create-bubble');

const groups = {}; // Object to hold groups

function getRandomColor() {
    const letters = '0123456789ABCDEF';
    let color = '#';
    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
        color += letters[Math.floor(Math.random() * 16)];
    }
    return color;
}
function getGroupPosition(group) {
    return group.getBoundingClientRect(); // Get the current position and size of the group
}
function createGroup(name, color) {
    const groupDiv = document.createElement('div');
    groupDiv.classList.add('group');
    groupDiv.style.border = `2px solid ${color}`; // Set border color
    groupDiv.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent'; // No fill
    groupDiv.style.padding = '10px'; // Add some padding
    groupDiv.style.margin = '10px'; // Add some margin for spacing

    const groupTitle = document.createElement('h3');
    groupTitle.innerText = name;
    groupTitle.style.marginBottom = '10px'; // Add some space below the title
    groupDiv.appendChild(groupTitle);

    // Only align bubbles if there are already bubbles in the group


    return groupDiv; // Return the group element
}

function createBubble() {
    const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!groupName) return;

    let group = groups[groupName];

    if (!group) {
        const color = getRandomColor(); // Generate a new color for the group
        group = createGroup(groupName, color);
        groups[groupName] = group; // Store the group in the groups object
        document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group); // Add the group to the container
    }

    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');
    newBubble.classList.add('bubble');
    newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.style.borderColor; // Set the bubble color
    newBubble.style.width = '50px';
    newBubble.style.height = '50px';
    newBubble.style.borderRadius = '10px'; // Rounded corners
    newBubble.style.margin = '5px'; // Spacing between bubbles
    newBubble.style.position = 'absolute'; // Ensure bubbles can be positioned
    newBubble.style.cursor = 'move'; // Change cursor to indicate draggable
    
    // Set a random initial position for the bubble
    newBubble.style.left = `${Math.random() * (window.innerWidth - 50)}px`; // Random position
    newBubble.style.top = `${Math.random() * (window.innerHeight - 50)}px`; // Random position

    // Create a span for editable text
    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
    textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit"; // Default text
    textSpan.style.display = 'block'; // Display block for line breaks
    textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center'; // Center text

    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan); // Add the text span to the bubble
    document.body.appendChild(newBubble); // Append bubble to body for free movement

    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName; // Store the group name in a data attribute
    group.bubbles.push(newBubble); // Ensure this line is executed
    group.element.appendChild(newBubble); // Ensure bubbles are added to the correct group

    // Make the bubble editable
    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);

    // Call functions for dragging
    makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);
    console.log(JSON.stringify(groups, null, 2));
    callBack([...document.querySelectorAll('.group')]);
}

function callBack() {
    Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {
        const group = groups[groupName];
        const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element); // Get the new position of the group
        
        group.bubbles.forEach(bubble => {
            // Move each bubble to align with the new group position
            moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition);
        });
    });
}

function moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition) {
    bubble.style.left = `${groupPosition.left + 20}px`; // Example positioning logic
    bubble.style.top = `${groupPosition.top + 50}px`; // Example positioning logic
}

function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {
    textSpan.addEventListener('click', function () {
        const inputField = document.createElement('input');
        inputField.type = 'text';
        inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  // Set the input's value to current text
        textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  // Replace text with input field
        inputField.focus();  // Automatically focus on the input

        inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {
            updateText();
        });

        // Listen for the Enter key
        inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                updateText();
            }
        });

        function updateText() {
            textSpan.innerText = inputField.value || "Click to Edit";  // Update textSpan with new input value
            inputField.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Replace input with updated text
        }
    });
}

function makeBubbleDraggable(bubble) {
    let offsetX, offsetY;

    bubble.addEventListener('mousedown', function (event) {
        offsetX = event.clientX - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().left; // Calculate horizontal offset
        offsetY = event.clientY - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().top; // Calculate vertical offset
        
        // Bring the bubble to the front when dragging
        bubble.style.zIndex = 1000;

        function mouseMoveHandler(e) {
            bubble.style.left = `${e.clientX - offsetX}px`; // Use the offset
            bubble.style.top = `${e.clientY - offsetY}px`; // Use the offset
        }

        function mouseUpHandler() {
            // Stop listening for the dragging events
            document.removeEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);
            document.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);

            // Call the callback function after dragging ends
            callBack(); // This can snap the bubble back to its group if needed

            // Reset z-index when done dragging
            bubble.style.zIndex = ''; 
        }

        document.addEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);
        document.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);
    });
}





document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    document.getElementById('create-bubble').addEventListener('click', createBubble);

    // Add keyboard event listener for Ctrl + B
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function (e) {
        if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'b') {
            e.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default browser action
            createBubble(); // Call createBubble function
        }
    });
});

const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');
const createBubbleBtn = document.getElementById('create-bubble');

const groups = {}; // Object to hold groups

function getRandomColor() {
    const letters = '0123456789ABCDEF';
    let color = '#';
    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
        color += letters[Math.floor(Math.random() * 16)];
    }
    return color;
}
function getGroupPosition(group) {
    return group.getBoundingClientRect(); // Get the current position and size of the group
}
function createGroup(name, color) {
    const groupDiv = document.createElement('div');
    groupDiv.classList.add('group');
    groupDiv.style.border = `2px solid ${color}`;
    groupDiv.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent';
    groupDiv.style.padding = '10px';
    groupDiv.style.margin = '10px';

    const groupTitle = document.createElement('h3');
    groupTitle.innerText = name;
    groupDiv.appendChild(groupTitle);
    
    // Return an object with the group element and an empty bubbles array
    return { element: groupDiv, bubbles: [] };
}

function deleteGroup(groupName) {
    const group = groups[groupName]; // Find the group in the groups object

    if (!group) {
        alert(`Group '${groupName}' does not exist.`); // Show alert if the group is not found
        return;
    }

    // Remove all bubbles in the group
    group.bubbles.forEach(bubble => {
        bubble.remove(); // Remove the bubble from the DOM
    });

    // Remove the group element from the DOM
    group.element.remove();

    // Remove the group from the `groups` object
    delete groups[groupName];

    callBack();

    console.log(`Group '${groupName}' and its bubbles were deleted.`);
    alert(`Group '${groupName}' and its bubbles were deleted.`); // Show success message
}

function createBubble() {
    const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!groupName) return;

    let group = groups[groupName];

    if (!group) {
        const color = getRandomColor(); 
        group = createGroup(groupName, color); 
        groups[groupName] = group;
        document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element); 
        callBack();
    }

    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');
    newBubble.classList.add('bubble');
    newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor;

    newBubble.style.margin = '5px';
    newBubble.style.position = 'absolute';
    newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';
    
    const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element); // Get the group's position
    const bubbleXOffset = groupPosition.left + 20; // Position relative to the group
    const bubbleYOffset = groupPosition.top + 50; // Position relative to the group
    newBubble.style.left = `${bubbleXOffset}px`; // Set initial position within the group
    newBubble.style.top = `${bubbleYOffset}px`; // Set initial position within the group
    newBubble.style.zIndex = 1; // Initial z-index for bubbles

    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
    textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit";
    textSpan.style.display = 'block';
    textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center';

    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan);
    document.body.appendChild(newBubble); 

    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName; 
    group.bubbles.push(newBubble); 

    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);
    makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);
    callBack();
}


function callBack() {
    Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {
        const group = groups[groupName];
        const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);
        
        group.bubbles.forEach((bubble, index) => {
            moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index);
        });
    });
}

function moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index) {
    const bubbleWidth = bubble.offsetWidth; // Get the current width of the bubble
    const bubbleHeight = bubble.offsetHeight; // Get the current height of the bubble
    const marginTop = 60; // Space for the group title
    const spacing = 10; // Space between bubbles

    // Calculate the left position for the bubble
    const leftPosition = groupPosition.left + (bubbleWidth + spacing) * (index % Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing)));
    
    // Calculate the top position for the bubble
    const topPosition = groupPosition.top + marginTop + Math.floor(index / Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing))) * (bubbleHeight + spacing);

    bubble.style.left = `${leftPosition}px`;
    bubble.style.top = `${topPosition}px`;

    // Calculate how many bubbles can fit in a row
    const bubblesPerRow = Math.floor((groupPosition.width) / (bubbleWidth + spacing));
    
    // Calculate the x position to center bubbles
    const offsetX = (groupPosition.width - (bubblesPerRow * (bubbleWidth + spacing) - spacing)) / 2;

    // Calculate the x and y positions
    const xPosition = offsetX + (index % bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleWidth + spacing);
    const yPosition = Math.floor(index / bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleHeight + spacing) + marginTop;

    bubble.style.left = `${groupPosition.left + xPosition}px`;
    bubble.style.top = `${groupPosition.top + yPosition}px`;
}


function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {
    textSpan.addEventListener('click', function () {
        const inputField = document.createElement('input');
        inputField.type = 'text';
        inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  // Set the input's value to current text
        textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  // Replace text with input field
        inputField.focus();  // Automatically focus on the input

        inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {
            updateText();
        });

        // Listen for the Enter key
        inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                updateText();
            }
        });

        function updateText() {
            textSpan.innerText = inputField.value || "Click to Edit";  // Update textSpan with new input value
            inputField.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Replace input with updated text
        }
    });
}

function makeBubbleDraggable(bubble) {
    let offsetX, offsetY, originalGroup;

    bubble.addEventListener('mousedown', function (event) {
        offsetX = event.clientX - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().left;
        offsetY = event.clientY - bubble.getBoundingClientRect().top;
        originalGroup = bubble.dataset.group; // Store the original group

        // Bring the bubble to the front when dragging
        bubble.style.zIndex = 1000;

        function mouseMoveHandler(e) {
            bubble.style.left = `${e.clientX - offsetX}px`;
            bubble.style.top = `${e.clientY - offsetY}px`;
        }

        function mouseUpHandler(e) {
            // Stop listening for dragging events
            document.removeEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);
            document.removeEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);

            // Check for the group where the bubble is released
            const newGroupElement = document.elementFromPoint(e.clientX, e.clientY);

            if (newGroupElement && newGroupElement.classList.contains('group')) {
                const newGroupName = newGroupElement.querySelector('h3').innerText.trim().toLowerCase(); // Get the group name

                // If the bubble is dropped in a different group
                if (newGroupName !== originalGroup) {
                    // Remove the bubble from the original group
                    const originalGroupElement = groups[originalGroup].element;
                    originalGroupElement.removeChild(bubble); // Ensure this is the correct element

                    // Append the bubble to the new group
                    newGroupElement.appendChild(bubble);
                    bubble.dataset.group = newGroupName; // Update the group data attribute
                }
            }

            // Reset z-index when done dragging
            bubble.style.zIndex = '';
        }

        document.addEventListener('mousemove', mouseMoveHandler);
        document.addEventListener('mouseup', mouseUpHandler);
    });
}

        if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'b') {
            e.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default browser action
            createBubble(); // Call createBubble function
        }
    });

    contextMenu.style.top = `${event.pageY}px`;

function changeBubbleGroup(bubble, newGroup) {
    // Assuming each bubble has a reference to its current group
    const currentGroupName = bubble.currentGroup; // Adjust as per your structure

    // Find the current group
    const currentGroup = groups[currentGroupName];
    const newGroupData = groups[newGroup];

    if (!currentGroup || !newGroupData) {
        console.error('Invalid group specified.');
        return;
    }

    // Remove the bubble from the current group's child list
    const bubbleIndex = currentGroup.bubbles.indexOf(bubble);
    if (bubbleIndex > -1) {
        currentGroup.bubbles.splice(bubbleIndex, 1); // Remove from current group
        currentGroup.element.removeChild(bubble); // Remove from DOM if necessary
    }

    // Add the bubble to the new group's child list
    newGroupData.bubbles.push(bubble);
    newGroupData.element.appendChild(bubble); // Add to DOM if necessary

    // Update the bubble's current group reference
    bubble.currentGroup = newGroup; // Adjust as per your bubble structure

    console.log(`Moved bubble to group: ${newGroup}`);
}
