const createBubbleBtn = document.getElementById('create-bubble');

const groups = {}; // Object to hold groups

function getRandomColor() {
    const letters = '0123456789ABCDEF';
    let color = '#';
    for (let i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
        color += letters[Math.floor(Math.random() * 16)];
    }
    return color;
}
function getGroupPosition(group) {
    return group.getBoundingClientRect(); // Get the current position and size of the group
}
function createGroup(name, color) {
    const groupDiv = document.createElement('div');
    groupDiv.classList.add('group');
    groupDiv.style.border = `2px solid ${color}`;
    groupDiv.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent';
    groupDiv.style.padding = '10px';
    groupDiv.style.margin = '10px';

    const groupTitle = document.createElement('h3');
    groupTitle.innerText = name;
    groupDiv.appendChild(groupTitle);
    console.log(groupDiv.children);
    // Return an object with the group element and an empty bubbles array
    return { element: groupDiv, bubbles: [] };
}

function deleteGroup(groupName) {
    const group = groups[groupName]; // Find the group in the groups object

    if (!group) {
        alert(`Group '${groupName}' does not exist.`); // Show alert if the group is not found
        return;
    }

    // Remove all bubbles in the group
    group.bubbles.forEach(bubble => {
        bubble.remove(); // Remove the bubble from the DOM
    });

    // Remove the group element from the DOM
    group.element.remove();

    // Remove the group from the `groups` object
    delete groups[groupName];

    callBack();

    console.log(`Group '${groupName}' and its bubbles were deleted.`);
    alert(`Group '${groupName}' and its bubbles were deleted.`); // Show success message
}

function createBubble() {
    const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!groupName) return;

    let group = groups[groupName];

    if (!group) {
        const color = getRandomColor(); 
        group = createGroup(groupName, color); 
        groups[groupName] = group;
        document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element); 
        callBack();
    }
    
    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');
    newBubble.currentGroup = groupName;
    console.log(newBubble.currentGroup);
    newBubble.classList.add('bubble');
    newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor;


    newBubble.style.margin = '5px';
    newBubble.style.position = 'absolute';
    newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';
    
    const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element); // Get the group's position
    const bubbleXOffset = groupPosition.left + 20; // Position relative to the group
    const bubbleYOffset = groupPosition.top + 50; // Position relative to the group
    newBubble.style.left = `${bubbleXOffset}px`; // Set initial position within the group
    newBubble.style.top = `${bubbleYOffset}px`; // Set initial position within the group
    newBubble.style.zIndex = 1; // Initial z-index for bubbles

    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
    textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit";
    textSpan.style.display = 'block';
    textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center';

    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan);
    document.body.appendChild(newBubble); 

    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName; 
    group.bubbles.push(newBubble); 

    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);
    makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);
    callBack();

}


function callBack() {
    Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {
        const group = groups[groupName];
        const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);
        group.bubbles.forEach((bubble, index) => {
            moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index);
        });
    });
}

function moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index) {
    const bubbleWidth = bubble.offsetWidth; // Get the current width of the bubble
    const bubbleHeight = bubble.offsetHeight; // Get the current height of the bubble
    const marginTop = 60; // Space for the group title
    const spacing = 10; // Space between bubbles

    // Calculate the left position for the bubble
    const leftPosition = groupPosition.left + (bubbleWidth + spacing) * (index % Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing)));
    
    // Calculate the top position for the bubble
    const topPosition = groupPosition.top + marginTop + Math.floor(index / Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing))) * (bubbleHeight + spacing);

    bubble.style.left = `${leftPosition}px`;
    bubble.style.top = `${topPosition}px`;

    // Calculate how many bubbles can fit in a row
    const bubblesPerRow = Math.floor((groupPosition.width) / (bubbleWidth + spacing));
    
    // Calculate the x position to center bubbles
    const offsetX = (groupPosition.width - (bubblesPerRow * (bubbleWidth + spacing) - spacing)) / 2;

    // Calculate the x and y positions
    const xPosition = offsetX + (index % bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleWidth + spacing);
    const yPosition = Math.floor(index / bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleHeight + spacing) + marginTop;

    bubble.style.left = `${groupPosition.left + xPosition}px`;
    bubble.style.top = `${groupPosition.top + yPosition}px`;
}


function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {
    textSpan.addEventListener('click', function () {
        const inputField = document.createElement('input');
        inputField.type = 'text';
        inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;  // Set the input's value to current text
        textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);  // Replace text with input field
        inputField.focus();  // Automatically focus on the input

        inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {
            updateText();
        });

        // Listen for the Enter key
        inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                updateText();
            }
        });

        function updateText() {
            textSpan.innerText = inputField.value || "Click to Edit";  // Update textSpan with new input value
            inputField.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Replace input with updated text
        }
    });
}


function makeBubbleDraggable(bubbleElement) {
    let isDragging = false;
    let offsetX, offsetY;

    bubbleElement.addEventListener('mousedown', (event) => {
        isDragging = true;
        offsetX = event.clientX - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left;
        offsetY = event.clientY - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top;
        bubbleElement.style.position = 'absolute';  // Ensure it's positioned absolutely
    });
    
    document.addEventListener('mousemove', (event) => {
        if (isDragging) {
            console.log(bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left,bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top );
            const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');
            const containerRect = bubbleContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
            
            bubbleElement.style.left = `${event.clientX - offsetX}px`;
            bubbleElement.style.top = `${event.clientY -  offsetY}px`;
        }
    });

    document.addEventListener('mouseup', (event) => {
        if (isDragging) {
            isDragging = false;

            // Check for collision with groups
            Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {
                const group = groups[groupName];
                const groupRect = group.element.getBoundingClientRect();
                
                // Check if the bubble is dropped within the group
                if (
                    event.clientX >= groupRect.left &&
                    event.clientX <= groupRect.right &&
                    event.clientY >= groupRect.top &&
                    event.clientY <= groupRect.bottom
                ) {
                    changeBubbleGroup(bubbleElement, groupName, event.clientX, event.clientY); // Ensure groupName is passed correctly
                }
            });
        }
    });
}


function changeBubbleGroup(bubble, newGroupName, xdim, ydim) {
    const currentGroupName = bubble.currentGroup;
    const currentGroup = groups[currentGroupName];
    const newGroup = groups[newGroupName];

    if (!currentGroup || !newGroup) {
        console.error('Invalid group specified.');
        return;
    }

    // Get the bubble's current position before removing it
    const bubbleRect = bubble.getBoundingClientRect();
    const groupRect = newGroup.element.getBoundingClientRect();

    // Calculate the offset of the bubble relative to the viewport
    const offsetX = bubbleRect.left - window.scrollX; // Correct for window scroll
    const offsetY = bubbleRect.top - window.scrollY;  // Correct for window scroll

    // Remove the bubble from the current group's child list
    const bubbleIndex = currentGroup.bubbles.indexOf(bubble);
    if (bubbleIndex > -1) {
        currentGroup.bubbles.splice(bubbleIndex, 1);
        currentGroup.element.removeChild(bubble); // Ensure bubble is a child of currentGroup.element
    }

    // Add the bubble to the new group's child list
    newGroup.bubbles.push(bubble);
    newGroup.element.appendChild(bubble); // Add bubble to new group

    // Set the bubble's position relative to the new group
    // bubble.style.left = `${xdim}px`; // Adjust left position
    // bubble.style.top = `${ydim}px`;   // Adjust top position

    // Update the bubble's current group reference
    bubble.currentGroup = newGroupName;

    console.log(`Moved bubble to group: ${newGroupName}`);
}

        if (e.ctrlKey && e.key === 'b') {

// Function to show custom context menu
function showContextMenu(event, bubble) {
    event.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default right-click menu
    targetBubble = bubble; // Set the target bubble
    contextMenu.style.left = `${event.pageX}px`;
    contextMenu.style.top = `${event.pageY}px`;
    contextMenu.style.display = 'block';
}

    }
});

    const bubbleWidth = bubble.offsetWidth; // Get the current width of the bubble

Heres the create bubble function if you notice anything weird here

function createBubble() {
    const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!groupName) return;

    let group = groups[groupName];

    // Create group if it doesn't exist
    if (!group) {
        const color = getRandomColor(); 
        group = createGroup(groupName, color); 
        groups[groupName] = group;
        document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element); // Append the group itself to the bubble-container
        callBack();
    }
    
    // Create a new bubble
    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');
    console.log(newBubble.currentGroup);
    newBubble.classList.add('bubble');
    newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor; // Style the bubble to match the group's color

    newBubble.style.margin = '5px';
    newBubble.style.position = 'absolute'; // Ensure the bubble is positioned absolutely relative to the container
    newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';
    
    // Position the bubble relative to the group, but it will be a child of the bubble container
    const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element); // Get the group's position
    const bubbleXOffset = groupPosition.left + 20; // Position relative to the group
    const bubbleYOffset = groupPosition.top + 50; // Position relative to the group
    newBubble.style.left = `${bubbleXOffset}px`; // Set initial position relative to the group (but within the overall container)
    newBubble.style.top = `${bubbleYOffset}px`; 
    newBubble.style.zIndex = 1; // Initial z-index for bubbles

    // Add editable text to the bubble
    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
    textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit";
    textSpan.style.display = 'block';
    textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center';
    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan);

    // Append the bubble directly to the bubble container (NOT the group element)
    const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');
    bubbleContainer.appendChild(newBubble);

    // Associate the bubble with the group via data attribute, NOT DOM structure
    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName; 
    group.bubbles.push(newBubble); // Add the bubble to the group's logical list of bubbles

    // Make the bubble editable and draggable
    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);
    makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);

    callBack(); // Trigger any necessary callbacks after the bubble is created
}

2024-09-28 19:43:21 | Something isn't working with how the text is being referenced inside the bubble. Can you read how the text is being stored and help me access it better?

function createBubble() {
    const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!groupName) return;

    let group = groups[groupName];

    // Create group if it doesn't exist
    if (!group) {
        const color = getRandomColor(); 
        group = createGroup(groupName, color); 
        groups[groupName] = group;
        document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element); 
        callBack();
    }
    
    // Create a new bubble
    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');
    newBubble.classList.add('bubble');
    newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor; 

    newBubble.style.margin = '5px';
    newBubble.style.position = 'absolute';
    newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';
    
    const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);
    const bubbleXOffset = groupPosition.left + 20;
    const bubbleYOffset = groupPosition.top + 50;
    newBubble.style.left = `${bubbleXOffset}px`;
    newBubble.style.top = `${bubbleYOffset}px`; 
    newBubble.style.zIndex = 1;

    // Add editable text to the bubble
    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
    textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit";
    textSpan.style.display = 'block';
    textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center';
    textSpan.style.zIndex = '10'; // Ensure the text span is on top and clickable

    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan);

    const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');
    bubbleContainer.appendChild(newBubble);

    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName; 
    group.bubbles.push(newBubble);

    // Add bubble edit and drag functionality
    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);
    makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);

    callBack(); 
}




function callBack() {
    Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {
        const group = groups[groupName];
        const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);
        group.bubbles.forEach((bubble, index) => {
            moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index);
        });
    });
}

function moveBubbleToGroup(bubble, groupPosition, index) {
    const bubbleWidth = bubble.offsetWidth; // Get the current width of the bubble
    const bubbleHeight = bubble.offsetHeight; // Get the current height of the bubble
    const marginTop = 60; // Space for the group title
    const spacing = 10; // Space between bubbles

    // Calculate the left position for the bubble
    const leftPosition = groupPosition.left + (bubbleWidth + spacing) * (index % Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing)));
    
    // Calculate the top position for the bubble
    const topPosition = groupPosition.top + marginTop + Math.floor(index / Math.floor((groupPosition.width - spacing) / (bubbleWidth + spacing))) * (bubbleHeight + spacing);

    bubble.style.left = `${leftPosition}px`;
    bubble.style.top = `${topPosition}px`;

    // Calculate how many bubbles can fit in a row
    const bubblesPerRow = Math.floor((groupPosition.width) / (bubbleWidth + spacing));
    
    // Calculate the x position to center bubbles
    const offsetX = (groupPosition.width - (bubblesPerRow * (bubbleWidth + spacing) - spacing)) / 2;

    // Calculate the x and y positions
    const xPosition = offsetX + (index % bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleWidth + spacing);
    const yPosition = Math.floor(index / bubblesPerRow) * (bubbleHeight + spacing) + marginTop;

    bubble.style.left = `${groupPosition.left + xPosition}px`;
    bubble.style.top = `${groupPosition.top + yPosition}px`;
    
}


function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {
    textSpan.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
        event.stopPropagation();  // Prevent click events from affecting other elements

        const inputField = document.createElement('input');
        inputField.type = 'text';
        inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;
        inputField.style.zIndex = '20';  // Ensure the input is on top

        textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);
        inputField.focus();

        // Disable dragging while editing
        bubble.draggable = false;
        inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {
            setTimeout(() => {
                updateText(inputField, bubble);
            }, 0); // Delay by 0ms to ensure the 'keydown' event completes first
        });

        inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                updateText(inputField, bubble);
            }
        });

    });

    function updateText(inputElement, bubble) {
        const newValue = inputElement.value.trim();

        if (newValue) {
            const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
            textSpan.innerText = newValue;
            textSpan.classList.add('bubble-text');

            // Ensure the input element is still part of the DOM
            if (inputElement.parentNode) {
                inputElement.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Only replace if the input is still in the DOM
            }

            // Rebind the click event for editing
            makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan);
        }

        // Enable dragging again
        bubble.draggable = true;
    }
}

2024-09-28 19:53:40 | // Function to collect bubble data from the DOM
function getBubbleData() {
    let bubbles = document.querySelectorAll('.bubble'); // Assuming bubbles have a class 'bubble'
    let bubbleData = [];

    bubbles.forEach(bubble => {
        const group = bubble.dataset.group;  // Assuming groups are stored in a data attribute
        const textSpan = bubble.querySelector('.bubble-text');  // Find the child textspan within the bubble
        console.log(group, textSpan);
        if (textSpan) {
            const text = textSpan.innerText;  // Get the text from the textspan
            bubbleData.push({ group, text });
        }
    });

    return bubbleData;
}


// Function to save bubbles
function saveBubbles() {
    const bubbles = getBubbleData();
    console.log(bubbles);
    fetch('/saveBubbles', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json'
        },
        body: JSON.stringify({ bubbles })
    })
    .then(response => response.json())
    .then(data => {
        if (data.success) {
            alert("Bubbles saved successfully!");
        } else {
            alert("Error saving bubbles.");
        }
    })
    .catch(error => {
        console.error("Error:", error);
    });
}

// Call saveBubbles when the user clicks the save button
document.getElementById('saveButton').addEventListener('click', saveBubbles);



This is the save stuff in the index.js

// Route to save bubble DOM structure to SQL database
app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.session.userId;  // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session
  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles;

  if (!userId || !bubbles) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });
  }

  try {
      // Connect to the database
      await sql.connect(config);

      // Insert each bubble into the database
      for (const bubble of bubbles) {
          const { group, text } = bubble;

          const query = `
              INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, group)
              VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)
          `;

          const request = new sql.Request();
          request.input('userId', sql.Int, userId);
          request.input('text', sql.NVarChar, text);
          request.input('group', sql.NVarChar, group);

          await request.query(query);
      }

      res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (error) {
      console.error("Database error:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });
  }
});

app.get('/bubbles', (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles', 'index.html'));
    } catch (err) {
      res.redirect('/login');
    }
  } else {
    res.redirect('/login');
  }
});

// Route to save bubble DOM structure to SQL database
app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.session.userId;  // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session
  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles;
  console.log(userId, bubbles);
  if (!userId || !bubbles) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });
  }

  try {
      // Connect to the database
      await sql.connect(config);

      // Insert each bubble into the database
      for (const bubble of bubbles) {
          const { group, text } = bubble;

          const query = `
              INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, group)
              VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)
          `;

          const request = new sql.Request();
          request.input('userId', sql.Int, userId);
          request.input('text', sql.NVarChar, text);
          request.input('group', sql.NVarChar, group);

          await request.query(query);
      }

      res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (error) {
      console.error("Database error:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });
  }
});

// Route to load user's saved bubbles from SQL database
app.get('/loadBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      const username = decoded.username;
      await sql.connect(config);
      const result = await sql.query`SELECT bubbles FROM Users WHERE username = ${username}`;
      res.json(result.recordset[0].bubbles);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.status(500).send('Failed to load bubbles.');
    }
  } else {
    res.status(401).send('Unauthorized.');
  }
});

// Serve the login page
app.get('/login', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));
});


// Route to retrieve and print Users table
app.get('/users', async (req, res) => {
  try {
      // Connect to the database
      await sql.connect(config);
      
      // Query to select all users
      const result = await sql.query`SELECT * FROM Users`;

      // Log the results to the console
      console.log(result.recordset);

      // Send the results as a response
      res.json(result.recordset);
  } catch (error) {
      console.error("Database error:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving users.' });
  }
});

Here's the code for createBubble() to reference the normal way of creating a bubble

function createBubble() {
    const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!groupName) return;

    let group = groups[groupName];

    // Create group if it doesn't exist
    if (!group) {
        const color = getRandomColor(); 
        group = createGroup(groupName, color); 
        groups[groupName] = group;
        document.getElementById('bubble-container').appendChild(group.element); 
        callBack();
    }
    
    // Create a new bubble
    const newBubble = document.createElement('div');
    newBubble.classList.add('bubble');
    newBubble.style.backgroundColor = group.element.style.borderColor; 

    newBubble.style.margin = '5px';
    newBubble.style.position = 'absolute';
    newBubble.style.cursor = 'move';
    
    const groupPosition = getGroupPosition(group.element);
    const bubbleXOffset = groupPosition.left + 20;
    const bubbleYOffset = groupPosition.top + 50;
    newBubble.style.left = `${bubbleXOffset}px`;
    newBubble.style.top = `${bubbleYOffset}px`; 
    newBubble.style.zIndex = 1;

    // Add editable text to the bubble
    const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
    textSpan.innerText = "Click to Edit";
    textSpan.style.display = 'block';
    textSpan.style.textAlign = 'center';
    textSpan.style.zIndex = '10'; // Ensure the text span is on top and clickable

    newBubble.appendChild(textSpan);

    const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');
    bubbleContainer.appendChild(newBubble);

    newBubble.dataset.group = groupName; 
    group.bubbles.push(newBubble);

    // Add bubble edit and drag functionality
    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);
    makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);

    callBack(); 
}

  try {
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    await sql.connect(config);
    await sql.query`INSERT INTO Users (username, password) VALUES (${username}, ${hashedPassword})`;

// User login route
app.post('/login', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    await sql.connect(config);
    const result = await sql.query`SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = ${username}`;
    if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
      const user = result.recordset[0];
      const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);
      if (passwordMatch) {
        const token = jwt.sign({ username: user.username, id: user.id }, JWT_SECRET);
        req.session.userId = user.id; // Store user ID in session
        res.cookie('authToken', token);
        res.redirect('/bubbles');
      } else {
        res.status(400).send('Invalid password.');
      }
    } else {
      res.status(400).send('User not found.');
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    res.status(500).send('Login failed.');
  }
});

// Route to serve the bubble site after login
app.get('/bubbles', (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles', 'index.html'));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.redirect('/login');
    }
  } else {
    res.redirect('/login');
  }
});

// Route to save bubble DOM structure to SQL database
app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.session.userId; // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session
  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles; // Expecting bubbles to be an array of objects
  console.log(userId, bubbles);

  if (!userId || !Array.isArray(bubbles)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });
  }

  try {
    await sql.connect(config);
    // Clear existing bubbles for this user if needed (optional)
    await sql.query`DELETE FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = ${userId}`;

    // Insert each bubble into the database
    for (const bubble of bubbles) {
      const { group, text } = bubble;
      const query = `
          INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, [group]) 
          VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)
      `;
      const request = new sql.Request();
      request.input('userId', sql.Int, userId);
      request.input('text', sql.NVarChar, text);
      request.input('group', sql.NVarChar, group);
      await request.query(query);
    }

    res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });
  }
});

// Endpoint to load user's bubbles
app.get('/loadBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      const userId = decoded.userId; // Assuming userId is included in your token
      const bubblesResult = await sql.query`SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = ${userId}`;

      res.json({
        success: true,
        bubbles: bubblesResult.recordset // Send the user's bubbles
      });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Internal server error' });
    }
  } else {
    res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
});


// Serve the login page
app.get('/login', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));
});

// Route to retrieve and print Users table
app.get('/users', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    await sql.connect(config);
    const result = await sql.query`SELECT * FROM Users`;
    console.log(result.recordset);
    res.json(result.recordset);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving users.' });
  }
});

// Route to retrieve all bubbles associated with user with id=3
app.get('/userbubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = 3; // You can replace this with a dynamic value if needed

  try {
      // Connect to the database
      await sql.connect(config);

      // Query to select all bubbles for the specified user
      const result = await sql.query`SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = ${userId}`;

      // Check if any bubbles were found
      if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
          // Send the bubbles as a response
          res.json(result.recordset);
      } else {
          res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'No bubbles found for this user.' });
      }
  } catch (error) {
      console.error("Database error:", error);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving bubbles.' });
  }
});


// Start the server
const port = 3000;
app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server running at http://localhost:${port}`);
});

    const groupName = prompt("Enter the group name for this bubble:").trim().toLowerCase();

    group.bubbles.push(newBubble);

    // Add bubble edit and drag functionality
    makeBubbleEditable(newBubble, textSpan);
    makeBubbleDraggable(newBubble);

    callBack(); 
}
function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {
    textSpan.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
        event.stopPropagation();  // Prevent click events from affecting other elements

        const inputField = document.createElement('input');
        inputField.type = 'text';
        inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;
        inputField.style.zIndex = '20';  // Ensure the input is on top

        textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);
        inputField.focus();

        // Disable dragging while editing
        bubble.draggable = false;
        inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {
            setTimeout(() => {
                updateText(inputField, bubble);
            }, 0); // Delay by 0ms to ensure the 'keydown' event completes first
        });

        inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                updateText(inputField, bubble);
            }
        });

    });

    function updateText(inputElement, bubble) {
        const newValue = inputElement.value.trim();

        if (newValue) {
            const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
            textSpan.innerText = newValue;
            textSpan.classList.add('bubble-text');

            // Ensure the input element is still part of the DOM
            if (inputElement.parentNode) {
                inputElement.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Only replace if the input is still in the DOM
            }

            // Rebind the click event for editing
            makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan);
        }

        // Enable dragging again
        bubble.draggable = true;
    }
}

So when a bubble is initialized originally, the 'click to edit' text is not saved in the DOM in the same way. It is saved like this:

but once an edit is made, or even if the text is clicked on, it begins to be referenced in the DOM like this:

<span class="bubble-text">asdfto Edit</span>

which is what I want. Why would it be the other way and how could I fix that?

let targetBubble = null; // Variable to store the current bubble

// Function to show custom context menu
function showContextMenu(event, bubble) {
    event.preventDefault(); // Prevent the default right-click menu
    targetBubble = bubble; // Set the target bubble
    contextMenu.style.left = `${event.pageX}px`;
    contextMenu.style.top = `${event.pageY}px`;
    contextMenu.style.display = 'block';
}

// Event listener for deleting the bubble
document.getElementById('delete-bubble-btn').addEventListener('click', function() {
    if (targetBubble) {
        targetBubble.remove(); // Delete the bubble
        contextMenu.style.display = 'none'; // Hide the menu
    }
});

// Hide context menu if clicked anywhere else
document.addEventListener('click', function() {
    contextMenu.style.display = 'none';
});

function makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan) {
    textSpan.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
        event.stopPropagation();  // Prevent click events from affecting other elements

        const inputField = document.createElement('input');
        inputField.type = 'text';
        inputField.value = textSpan.innerText;
        inputField.style.zIndex = '20';  // Ensure the input is on top

        textSpan.replaceWith(inputField);
        inputField.focus();

        // Disable dragging while editing
        bubble.draggable = false;
        inputField.addEventListener('blur', function () {
            setTimeout(() => {
                updateText(inputField, bubble);
            }, 0); // Delay by 0ms to ensure the 'keydown' event completes first
        });

        inputField.addEventListener('keydown', function (event) {
            if (event.key === 'Enter') {
                updateText(inputField, bubble);
            }
        });

    });

    function updateText(inputElement, bubble) {
        const newValue = inputElement.value.trim();

        if (newValue) {
            const textSpan = document.createElement('span');
            textSpan.innerText = newValue;
            textSpan.classList.add('bubble-text');

            // Ensure the input element is still part of the DOM
            if (inputElement.parentNode) {
                inputElement.replaceWith(textSpan);  // Only replace if the input is still in the DOM
            }

            // Rebind the click event for editing
            makeBubbleEditable(bubble, textSpan);
        }

        // Enable dragging again
        bubble.draggable = true;
    }
}


function makeBubbleDraggable(bubbleElement) {
    let isDragging = false;
    let offsetX, offsetY;

    bubbleElement.addEventListener('mousedown', (event) => {
        isDragging = true;
        offsetX = event.clientX - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left;
        offsetY = event.clientY - bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top;
        bubbleElement.style.position = 'absolute';  // Ensure it's positioned absolutely
    });
    
    document.addEventListener('mousemove', (event) => {
        if (isDragging) {
            // console.log(bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().left,bubbleElement.getBoundingClientRect().top );
            const bubbleContainer = document.getElementById('bubble-container');
            const containerRect = bubbleContainer.getBoundingClientRect();
            const scrollX = window.scrollX || document.documentElement.scrollLeft;
            const scrollY = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop;


            bubbleElement.style.left = (event.clientX - offsetX + scrollX) + 'px';
            bubbleElement.style.top = (event.clientY - offsetY + scrollY -30) + 'px'
        }
    });

    document.addEventListener('mouseup', (event) => {
        if (isDragging) {
            isDragging = false;

            // Check for collision with groups
            Object.keys(groups).forEach(groupName => {
                const group = groups[groupName];
                const groupRect = group.element.getBoundingClientRect();
                
                // Check if the bubble is dropped within the group
                if (
                    event.clientX >= groupRect.left &&
                    event.clientX <= groupRect.right &&
                    event.clientY >= groupRect.top &&
                    event.clientY <= groupRect.bottom
                ) {
                    changeBubbleGroup(bubbleElement, groupName, event.clientX - offsetX, event.clientY -  offsetY); // Ensure groupName is passed correctly
                }
            });
        }
        
    });
}

2024-09-30 19:52:21 | const express = require('express');
const session = require('express-session');
const sql = require('mssql');
const path = require('path');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const cookieParser = require('cookie-parser');

const app = express();

// Middleware for handling POST data
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));
app.use(express.json());
app.use(cookieParser()); // Middleware to parse cookies

// Serve static files from bubbleSiteFiles directory
app.use('/bubbles', express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles')));

require('dotenv').config();

// SQL Server configuration
const poolConfig = {
  user: process.env.DB_USER,              // Use environment variable
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,      // Use environment variable
  server: process.env.DB_SERVER,          // Use environment variable
  database: process.env.DB_DATABASE,      // Use environment variable
  options: {
    encrypt: true, // Set to true if using Azure
    trustServerCertificate: false, // Set to true for local testing, if necessary
    enableArithAbort: true, // Required for Azure SQL
  },
};

// JWT secret key
const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET; // Use environment variable

// Create a connection pool
const poolPromise = new sql.ConnectionPool(poolConfig)
  .connect()
  .then(pool => {
    console.log('Connected to MSSQL');
    return pool;
  })
  .catch(err => {
    console.error('Database connection failed: ', err);
  });


// Session middleware setup
app.use(session({
  secret: JWT_SECRET, // Replace with your secret key
  resave: false,
  saveUninitialized: true,
  cookie: { secure: false } // Set to true if using HTTPS
}));

app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.redirect('/login'); // Redirects root URL to the login page
});

// User registration route
app.post('/register', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    await pool.request()
      .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)
      .input('hashedPassword', sql.NVarChar, hashedPassword)
      .query('INSERT INTO Users (username, password) VALUES (@username, @hashedPassword)');
    res.redirect('/login');
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    res.status(500).send('Registration failed.');
  }
});

// User login route
app.post('/login', async (req, res) => {
  const { username, password } = req.body;
  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request()
      .input('username', sql.NVarChar, username)
      .query('SELECT * FROM Users WHERE username = @username');
    if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
      const user = result.recordset[0];
      const passwordMatch = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password);
      if (passwordMatch) {
        const token = jwt.sign({ username: user.username, id: user.id }, JWT_SECRET);
        req.session.userId = user.id; // Store user ID in session
        res.cookie('authToken', token);
        res.redirect('/bubbles');
      } else {
        res.status(400).send('Invalid password.');
      }
    } else {
      res.status(400).send('User not found.');
    }
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(err);
    res.status(500).send('Login failed.');
  }
});

// Route to serve the bubble site after login
app.get('/bubbles', (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'bubbleSiteFiles', 'index.html'));
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.redirect('/login');
    }
  } else {
    res.redirect('/login');
  }
});

// Route to save bubble DOM structure to SQL database
app.post('/saveBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.session.userId; // Assuming user is logged in and userId is stored in the session
  const bubbles = req.body.bubbles; // Expecting bubbles to be an array of objects
  console.log(userId, bubbles);

  if (!userId || !Array.isArray(bubbles)) {
    return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Missing userId or bubbles data.' });
  }

  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    // Clear existing bubbles for this user if needed (optional)
    await pool.request()
      .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
      .query('DELETE FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

    // Insert each bubble into the database
    for (const bubble of bubbles) {
      const { group, text } = bubble;
      await pool.request()
        .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
        .input('text', sql.NVarChar, text)
        .input('group', sql.NVarChar, group)
        .query('INSERT INTO UserBubbles (userId, text, [group]) VALUES (@userId, @text, @group)');
    }

    res.json({ success: true });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error saving bubbles.' });
  }
});

// Endpoint to load user's bubbles
app.get('/loadBubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const token = req.cookies.authToken;
  if (token) {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      const userId = decoded.id; // Assuming userId is included in your token
      const pool = await poolPromise;
      const bubblesResult = await pool.request()
        .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
        .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

      res.json({
        success: true,
        bubbles: bubblesResult.recordset // Send the user's bubbles
      });
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Internal server error' });
    }
  } else {
    res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Unauthorized' });
  }
});

// Serve the login page
app.get('/login', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'public', 'index.html'));
});

// Route to retrieve and print Users table
app.get('/users', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request().query('SELECT * FROM Users');
    console.log(result.recordset);
    res.json(result.recordset);
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving users.' });
  }
});

// Route to retrieve all bubbles associated with user with id=3
app.get('/userbubbles', async (req, res) => {
  const userId = 3; // You can replace this with a dynamic value if needed

  try {
    const pool = await poolPromise;
    const result = await pool.request()
      .input('userId', sql.Int, userId)
      .query('SELECT * FROM UserBubbles WHERE userId = @userId');

    if (result.recordset.length > 0) {
      res.json(result.recordset);
    } else {
      res.status(404).json({ success: false, message: 'No bubbles found for this user.' });
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Database error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: 'Error retrieving bubbles.' });
  }
});

// Start the server
const port = 3000;
app.listen(port, () => {
  console.log(`Server running at http://localhost:${port}`);
});
